***vervuiling.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vervuiling.html>vervuiling</a> (13608)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vervulinge</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vervuilen.html>vervuilen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verwerren</i>, derived <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">werren</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:confuse.html>confuse</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:be.html>be</a> confused</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:originally.html>originally</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:strong.html>strong</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>verb</a>. Analysable <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:war.html>war</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:disorder.html>disorder</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:but.html>but</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:war.html>war</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">werre</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> deverbal. <p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijd.html>wijd</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verwijten.html>verwijten</a> (7260)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijten.html>wijten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blame.html>blame</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***verwonden.html

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verwonderen.html>verwonderen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verwondering.html>verwondering</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
